And special occasions and festivals somehow, always make the pain a little harder to bear. Perhaps because it’s hard to imagine what happiness could look like when the person who brought a smile to your face, can never be a part of your life again. 😢🥺

But still the memories you have with your Father👨‍👧♥️ will light up your life just as brightly as the Diwali diyas lit up home all these years.

I know It's really difficult to live without someone. But still you should be strong and brave to live through your life, carrying the memories and make your Father proud by achieving something great in life. 😇🙏🏻❤️

Because Memories with loved ones are all that matters. 🥰❤️

Wishing You a Blessful Day. ❤️😃

using namespace std;
void CreateArray(int arr[],int size){

    cout << "Enter the size of the array (Max 15):  \n" << endl;
    cin >> size;
    for (int i = 0; i < size; i++)
    {
        cout << "Enter the element : " << endl;
        cin >> arr[i];
    }
     
}

void DispArray(int arr[],int size){

    for (int i = 0; i < size; i++)
    {
        cout << arr[i];
    }
     
}

int main() {
    int size;
    int arr[15];

    cout << "Creating Array:" << CreateArray(arr,size);
    cout << "Displaying Array :" << DispArray(arr,size);

return 0;
}

31/12/2023, 3:43 pm - Manpreet Singh: *Ain't thou thee Lie*

_21/12/23_
*5:30PM*


It wasn't the day that mattered
Yet thou thee lives you scatterth

Madness ain't solution to everything
Brains don't, hearts that do ring 

It's not that easy to leave hands
Especially when held onto with golden strands

Love doesn't fade with the lies
Doesn't matter if it's the heart or the eyes

Many a lessons thou has learnth
Still some lessons you'd have to unearth 

Never take the path that maketh thee hurt
Ask thee heart if it's core or the crust 

You can't hold onto someone forever with thee hands
Either you'll burn yourself or burn the strands

Love's a lie everyone has thee told
Once broken hearts turnth cold

Lies of love ain't nothing to bribe 
It maketh you die whilst you survive

Be thankful for the love and trust you get
People will go, but it's the memories you can't forget.

void setup() {
  for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
    pinMode(ledPins[i], OUTPUT); // Set each LED pin as OUTPUT
  }
}

void loop() {
  for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
    digitalWrite(ledPins[i], HIGH); // Turn on the current LED
    delay(1000); // Wait for 1 second
    digitalWrite(ledPins[i], LOW); // Turn off the current LED

    if (i < 4) {
      delay(1000); // Wait for 1 second before turning on the next LED
    }
  }
}

31/01/2024, 10:30 am - Manpreet Singh: const int ledPins[] = {A0, A1, A2, A3, A4};
const int numLeds = 5;

void setup() {
  Serial.begin(9600);
  while (!Serial) {
    ;
  }

  for (int i = 0; i < numLeds; ++i) {
    pinMode(ledPins[i], OUTPUT);
  }
}

void loop() {
  if (Serial.available() > 0) {
    for (int i = 0; i < numLeds; ++i) {
      digitalWrite(ledPins[i], HIGH);
      delay(500);
      digitalWrite(ledPins[i], LOW);
    }
    delay(1000);
  }
}

void forward() {
  digitalWrite(5,HIGH);
  digitalWrite(6,LOW);
  digitalWrite(7,LOW);
  digitalWrite(8,HIGH);
}
void backward(){
  digitalWrite(5,LOW);
  digitalWrite(6,HIGH);
  digitalWrite(7,HIGH);
  digitalWrite(8,LOW);
}
 void left(){
  digitalWrite(5,HIGH);
  digitalWrite(6,LOW);
  digitalWrite(7,LOW);
  digitalWrite(8,LOW);
  }
void right(){
digitalWrite(5,LOW);
digitalWrite(6,LOW);
digitalWrite(7,LOW);
digitalWrite(8,HIGH);
}
void clockwise(){
digitalWrite(5,HIGH);
digitalWrite(6,LOW);
digitalWrite(7,HIGH);
digitalWrite(8,LOW);
}
void stopp()
{
digitalWrite(5,LOW);
digitalWrite(6,LOW);
digitalWrite(7,LOW);
digitalWrite(8,LOW);
}
